1. 机器学习的多分类问题可用的模型都有哪些？各优缺点是什么 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/343828523
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：图1.度量学习架构 四、选择适当的损失函数来训练大规模分类问题 本节我来介绍一组可用于训练大规模分类模型的损失函数。选择 正确的损失函数 在算法的成功中发挥关键作用。 对比损失（Contrastive …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

损失函数的选择对算法成功至关重要，因为它直接影响模型的训练效果和最终性能。对比损失函数通过度量样本之间的相对距离来训练模型，这种机制有助于优化模型的泛化能力，使其在未见过的数据上表现更佳。正确选择损失函数能够显著提升大规模分类模型的性能，从而确保模型不仅在训练集上表现良好，也能在实际应用中提供可靠的结果。因此，选择合适的损失函数是确保算法成功的关键步骤之一。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 损失函数的选择对算法成功至关重要。
  • 对比损失函数通过度量样本之间的相对距离来训练模型。
  • 正确选择损失函数能显著提升大规模分类模型的性能。
  • 对比损失函数有助于优化模型的泛化能力。

2. triplet loss稳定在margin附近? - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/365370142
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2023年12月6日 · 2，考虑有没有满足三元组挑选样本的条件，即选择K类样本，每类样本有N个图片，就是保证一个 batch_size 里面有正负样本可供挑选。 3、模型有没有区分度，如果模型太简单根本区分 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

batch_size的大小直接影响三元组样本的选择，进而对模型的训练过程产生重要影响。较大的batch_size能够提供更多的样本，有助于模型更好地学习特征，但同时也可能增加计算负担。模型的区分度是影响triplet loss稳定性的关键因素之一，较高的区分度意味着模型能够更有效地区分正样本、负样本和中性样本，从而使得triplet loss更加稳定。此外，margin值附近的区域是triplet loss稳定的原因之一，因为在这个区域内，模型能够更精确地调整正负样本之间的距离，从而提高模型的性能。因此，batch_size的选择、模型的区分度以及margin值的设置都是确保triplet loss稳定的重要因素。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • batch_size大小影响三元组样本的选择。
  • 模型的区分度会影响triplet loss的稳定性。
  • margin值附近是triplet loss稳定的原因。

3. 训练三元组损失无法收敛到margin以下，anchor和正、负 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/427795153
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2020年10月28日 · 具体实现的思路是：用具有较大margin的样本去修改模型，较少margin的三元组先不参与训练。 等较大margin的样本把模型训练差不多时，因为模型有更新，所以原来margin小的样本 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

在训练三元组损失时，较大的margin样本会先更新模型，因为这些样本更容易满足损失函数的要求。相比之下，较小margin的三元组样本则会在较大margin样本更新模型之后再参与训练。这种顺序可能导致较小margin的样本未能及时更新，从而使得损失无法进一步减小。因此，为了提高训练效果，需要确保较小margin的样本也能得到充分的更新，以促进整个模型的优化。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 训练三元组损失中的较大margin样本会先更新模型。
  • 较小margin的三元组样本会在较大margin样本更新模型之后再参与训练。
  • 训练过程中，较小margin的样本可能不会被及时更新，导致损失无法进一步减小。
正文（点击展开）

4. 深度学习领域的图文匹配任务为什么经常用三元组损失？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/530995258
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2022年5月2日 · 三元组损失（Triple loss），学习目标是相对距离，我们先思考图和图的匹配，直观上，两张图之间的相似性是可以用0~100来打分的，相似性可以度量，因此我们通过学习拉大基准样本 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

三元组损失是一种用于学习样本之间相对距离的损失函数，特别适用于图文匹配任务。通过这种损失函数，模型可以更准确地理解不同样本之间的相似度，相似性可以通过0到100的分数来表示。为了提高匹配精度，拉大基准样本与正样本或负样本之间的距离至关重要。因此，三元组损失能够有效提升模型对不同样本间相对距离的感知能力，从而在图文匹配任务中表现出更高的匹配精度。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 三元组损失用于学习样本之间的相对距离。
  • 三元组损失适用于图文匹配任务。
  • 相似性可以通过0~100的分数来表示。
  • 拉大基准样本与正样本或负样本之间的距离有助于提高匹配精度。
  • 三元组损失能够有效提升模型对不同样本间相对距离的感知能力。
正文（点击展开）

5. 应该怎么选择损失函数？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/439135524
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2023年2月5日 · Triplet loss 先从最经典的三元组 loss 说起， 三元组的构成：从训练数据集中随机选一个样本，该样本称为Anchor，然后再随机选取一个和Anchor属于同一类的样本和不同类的样本,这两个 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，三元组中的正样本与Anchor属于同一类，而负样本则与Anchor属于不同类。这种设置有助于模型学习区分同一类和不同类的特征。其次，选择合适的损失函数是关键步骤，需根据具体任务和数据特性进行调整。三元组损失通过对比Anchor与正负样本之间的距离来优化模型，从而提高分类准确性。此外，Anchor的选择对损失函数的表现有着重要影响，因此在训练过程中需要精心挑选合适的Anchor，以确保模型能够有效地学习到特征之间的差异。因此，通过合理设置三元组中的样本关系，并选择合适的损失函数和Anchor，可以显著提升模型的性能。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 三元组中的正样本与Anchor属于同一类。
  • 三元组中的负样本与Anchor属于不同类。
  • 选择损失函数需考虑具体任务和数据特性。
  • 三元组损失通过对比Anchor与正负样本的距离来优化模型。
  • Anchor的选择会影响损失函数的表现。
正文（点击展开）

6. 能否简单说明 PyTorch 所支持的损失函数定义与使用场景（选 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/468856872
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：问： 请查看Pytorch所支持的损失函数，并选择其中4个损失函数并解释说明每个损失函数的定义以及什么情况下需要用到它们。 接着，如题，此处选择：04-nn.CTCLoss、15-nn.HuberLoss、19 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

CTCLoss 专门用于处理序列数据，特别是在变长的文本或语音识别任务中，能够有效地处理包含不同长度序列的场景。相比之下，HuberLoss 则是一种结合了均方损失和绝对损失优点的损失函数，适用于数据中存在较大误差的情况，能够减少 outliers 的影响。因此，HuberLoss 在数据中存在较大误差时更为适用，而CTCLoss 则更适合处理序列长度不一的任务。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • CTCLoss 用于处理序列数据，特别是变长的文本或语音识别任务。
  • HuberLoss 结合了均方损失和绝对损失的优点，适用于减少 outliers 的影响。
  • CTCLoss 需要在处理包含不同长度序列的场景时使用。
  • HuberLoss 适用于数据中存在较大误差的情况。

7. 请问triplet loss 与二元交叉熵损失各自的优劣是什么，最好 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/402067053
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2020年9月6日 · 不过triplet loss的一个缺点是计算速度比cross-entropy loss慢，因为其要先构建筛选有效的三元组 (triplet)，再基于triplet进行计算，计算复杂度达到 O (N^3) 。 对于解决速度问题，CVPR19 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

triplet loss的计算复杂度较高，主要体现在构建有效的三元组耗时上。由于需要先筛选出有效的三元组，再基于这些三元组进行计算，这使得triplet loss的计算速度较慢。相比之下，二元交叉熵损失的计算速度较快，因为它不需要进行复杂的三元组筛选，直接基于分类任务进行计算。因此，三元组的筛选增加了计算时间，这也是triplet loss计算速度较慢的一个重要原因。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • triplet loss的计算复杂度较高；
  • 构建有效的三元组耗时；
  • 二元交叉熵损失计算速度较快；
  • triplet loss的计算速度较慢；
  • 三元组的筛选增加了计算时间。

19. 双线性插值的公式如何理解？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/53806569
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：双线性插值 双线性插值求解示意图 双线性插值是分别在两个方向（x, y）计算了共 3 次单线性插值，如下图所示，其中沿着 x 轴计算了 2 次，y 轴计算了 1 次 x,y 轴表示（横、纵两个方向的）坐标位置 z 轴 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

双线性插值是一种用于二维空间插值运算的方法，它首先在x轴方向进行两次线性插值，然后在y轴方向进行一次线性插值，总共进行了三次插值运算。这一过程确保了插值结果取决于x、y两个方向的坐标位置。具体而言，插值过程首先在x方向进行插值，得到中间结果，然后在y方向进行插值，最终确定插值点的值。因此，通过这种方式，双线性插值能够提供较为平滑且连续的图像处理效果。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 双线性插值在x轴方向进行了两次线性插值；
  • 双线性插值在y轴方向进行了一次线性插值；
  • 双线性插值总共进行了三次插值运算；
  • 双线性插值用于二维空间的插值运算；
  • 插值结果取决于x、y两个方向的坐标位置；
  • 插值过程先在x方向插值，再在y方向插值。
正文（点击展开）

正文

（知乎问题/专栏/想法页，正文未抓取，可点击上方链接阅读。）

  • 摘要：2019年7月4日 · 2. 线性插值Linear Interpolation——一阶插值法 线性插值是一种常见的数值插值方法，用于在已知数据点之间估算未知的函数值。 其基本思想是通过已知的两个数据点构建一条直线，然后 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

线性插值是一种通过已知的两个数据点构建直线来估算未知值的一阶插值方法，尽管其精度相对较低，但计算效率高，适用于简单插值任务。在网络结构中，反卷积作为常用的上采样方式，能够恢复特征图的尺寸，但在处理过程中可能引入较多噪声。因此，尽管线性插值在已知两个数据点间进行时表现良好，但在复杂场景下可能不够精确，无法处理更多点的情况。反卷积虽然能够有效上采样，但其恢复的特征图可能不够平滑，需要结合其他技术手段进行优化。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 线性插值通过已知的两个数据点构建一条直线来估算未知值。
  • 线性插值属于一阶插值法，精度较低但计算效率高。
  • 网络结构中特征融合时，反卷积是常用的一种上采样方式。
  • 线性插值仅在已知两个数据点间进行，无法处理更多点的情况。
  • 反卷积能够恢复特征图的尺寸，但可能引入较多噪声。
  • 线性插值适用于简单插值任务，但在复杂场景下可能不够精确。

21. Upsample、ConvTranspose2d、conv后PixelShuffle用法上有 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/342143752
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2021年1月30日 · Upsample: 无参数，仅依赖插值算法， 通过设定插值策略（如nearest邻近插值、bilinear双线性插值等）直接放大图像尺寸，输出仅依赖输入的空间维度缩放比例。 可能导致高频细 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Upsample操作不进行任何特征提取，仅通过放大图像尺寸来增加像素数量，但不会改变通道数。这一过程依赖于输入的空间维度缩放比例，而不涉及任何特征提取。在放大图像时，不同的插值策略会显著影响放大后的图像质量。其中，bilinear插值相比nearest邻近插值能够保留更多细节，因此在需要保持图像质量的情况下，bilinear插值是一个更好的选择。因此，选择合适的插值策略对于确保放大后的图像质量至关重要。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Upsample操作不进行任何特征提取，仅放大图像尺寸。
  • bilinear插值比nearest邻近插值能保留更多细节。
  • Upsample输出仅依赖输入的空间维度缩放比例。
  • Upsample不会改变通道数。
  • 插值策略影响放大后的图像质量。

22. u net 上采样如何实现的？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/346865980
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：医学图像分割方向，抛砖引玉回答一下： U-Net中上采样的目的是把低分辨率feature maps变成高分辨率的feature maps。想实现这个目的有两种方式 插值 的方法，比如最近邻插值，对每个像素复制两 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

插值方法在图像处理中扮演着重要角色，但同时也可能引入额外的噪声，影响图像的质量。具体而言，最近邻插值作为一种常见的插值方法，它不进行像素值的插值计算，而是直接使用最近的像素值进行填充，这虽然可以保持图像的原始细节，但可能无法平滑图像中的边缘，导致图像出现锯齿状的效果。此外，在上采样过程中，为了将低分辨率特征图放大至高分辨率，可能会损失部分低分辨率特征图中的重要信息，这进一步影响了图像的细节和整体质量。因此，选择合适的插值方法和策略对于保持图像质量和信息完整性至关重要。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 插值方法可能引入额外的噪声。
  • 最近邻插值不进行像素值的插值计算。
  • 上采样过程中可能会损失低分辨率特征图中的信息。

  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，三次样条插值通过B样条基函数实现，这种插值方法能够提供平滑的曲线，适用于多项数据点的拟合。其次，B样条基函数的平滑度与参数d相关，d越小，表示整型点越靠近插值点，权重越大。因此，d的大小直接影响了B样条基函数的平滑程度，进而影响了插值结果的光滑性和准确性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • d越小，表示整型点越靠近插值点，权重越大。
  • 三次样条插值通过B样条基函数实现。
  • B样条基函数的平滑度与d值相关。

24. 为什么很少有人用双线性插值来进行深度神经网络中的下采样 ...

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/335556776
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2019年7月18日 · 为什么很少有人用双线性插值来进行深度神经网络中的下采样操作？ 其他领域不说，至少图像分类领域，很多经典的网络结构如ResNet，都是用maxpool, avgpool或者stride = 2的卷积， …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

双线性插值不是深度神经网络下采样的常用方法，主要原因在于图像分类领域经典网络结构更偏好使用maxpool、avgpool或stride=2的卷积。其中，maxpool和avgpool操作比双线性插值更为常用，因为它们能够实现与双线性插值相同的功能，且具有更直观的优势。相比之下，双线性插值虽然能够实现下采样，但不如maxpool和avgpool直观，这使得maxpool和avgpool在实际应用中更为受欢迎。因此，尽管双线性插值在某些情况下可能适用，但在图像分类领域，maxpool和avgpool因其直观性和广泛应用性而更受欢迎。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 双线性插值不是深度神经网络下采样的常用方法。
  • 图像分类领域经典网络结构偏好使用maxpool、avgpool或stride=2的卷积。
  • maxpool和avgpool操作比双线性插值更常用。
  • stride=2的卷积可以实现与双线性插值相同的功能。
  • 双线性插值不如maxpool和avgpool直观。

25. 高分辨率遥感图像如何降采样为低分辨率遥感图像？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/32091500
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2015年7月13日 · 可以看到， ArcGIS 官方一共提供了 4 种栅格数据重采样的方法，分别是最邻近分配法（NEAREST）、众数算法（MAJORITY）、双线性插值法（BILINEAR）与三次卷积插值 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

栅格数据重采样是将高分辨率转为低分辨率的关键步骤，这一过程会直接影响降采样结果的质量。在这一过程中，不同的重采样方法会产生不同的效果。众数算法通过考虑像素的多数值来处理数据，而双线性插值法则使用周边四个像素值进行线性插值，这种方法能够提供较为平滑的结果。相比之下，三次卷积插值能够进一步提升结果的平滑度，提供更高质量的降采样图像。然而，最邻近分配法则直接取最近像素值，虽然操作简单，但可能会导致图像失真。因此，选择合适的重采样方法对于确保降采样结果的准确性和质量至关重要。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 栅格数据重采样方法会影响降采样结果。
  • 众数算法考虑了像素的多数值。
  • 双线性插值法使用了周边四个像素值进行线性插值。
  • 三次卷积插值能提供更平滑的结果。
  • 最邻近分配法直接取最近像素值，可能失真。
  • 栅格数据重采样是将高分辨率转为低分辨率的关键步骤。

  • 易漏细节梳理：

棋盘渲染是一种特殊的渲染技术，与线性插值、双线性插值和三线性插值等常规方法不同，它不是常用的常规渲染方法。尽管如此，棋盘渲染在某些特定场景中能够显著提高渲染效率，因此在需要优化渲染性能的情况下，它成为了一种值得考虑的选择。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 棋盘渲染是一种特殊的渲染技术。
  • 棋盘渲染与线性插值、双线性插值和三线性插值不同。
  • 棋盘渲染不是常用的常规渲染方法。
  • 棋盘渲染可能用于特定场景以提高渲染效率。

27. 插值算法能否缩小图片？ - 知乎

  • 链接：https://www.zhihu.com/question/57760258
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2017年3月31日 · 图片缩放这事儿，看似简单，实则暗藏杀机。 选错了插值算法，你辛苦拍的图放大后全是马赛克，缩小后又糊成一片。 我干开发20年，见过太多人因为一个参数没选对，整个项目的图像 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

插值算法的选择对图片质量有重大影响，尤其是在放大和缩小图片时。放大图片时，错误的插值算法会导致出现明显的马赛克，而缩小图片时则会导致图片变得模糊。因此，开发人员在处理图像时常常会因参数选择不当而导致图像质量下降。为了确保图像质量，开发人员需要仔细选择合适的插值算法，并根据具体需求调整相关参数。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 插值算法的选择对图片质量有重大影响。
  • 放大图片时错误的插值算法会导致出现马赛克。
  • 缩小图片时错误的插值算法会导致图片模糊。
  • 开发人员常因参数选择不当导致图像质量问题。

33. 深度系统如何查看各硬件驱动情况？- Community - Deepin ...

  • 链接：https://bbs.deepin.org/post/202738
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2020年9月24日 · 深度系统如何查看各硬件驱动情况？ 深度系统如何查看各硬件驱动情况？- Community - Deepin Technology Experiences and Insight 2119 views · 6 replies · Tofloor eva04 2020-09-24 00:34
  • 易漏细节梳理：

lspci和lsmod是Linux下的命令工具，lspci用于查看系统中的PCI设备，而lsmod则用于查看已加载的驱动模块。用户只需在终端中输入这些命令即可获取相关信息。然而，当前Linux设备管理器的功能相对有限，无法达到与Windows下设备管理器一样强大的程度，这使得用户在管理和诊断硬件问题时面临一定的挑战。因此，提升Linux设备管理器的功能，使其更加完善，是未来发展的方向之一。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • lspci和lsmod是Linux下的命令。
  • lspci用于查看PCI设备。
  • lsmod用于查看已加载的驱动模块。
  • 这些命令在终端中输入即可使用。
  • 设备管理器功能不完善。
  • 期待设备管理器能变得和Windows下的一样强大。

34. JAI functional contractions in relational metric spaces

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18515v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The 2015 fixed point result on rs-relational metric spaces due to Alam and Imdad [J. Fixed Point Th. Appl., 17 (2015), 693-702] is equivalent with the classical Banach Contraction Principle [Fund. Math., 3 (1922), 133-181]. This is also valid for the 1961 statement in metric spaces due to Edelstein [Proc. Amer. Math. Soc., 12 (1961), 7-10], or the 2005 fixed point result in quasi-ordered metric spaces obtained by Nieto and Rodriguez-Lopez [Order, 22 (2005), 223-239].
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Banach收缩原理在关系度量空间中成立，而Edelstein在1961年的陈述等价于这一原理。Nieto和Rodriguez-Lopez在2005年的研究则是在拟有序度量空间中进行的，这表明固定点结果在不同类型的度量空间中具有广泛适用性。Rs-关系度量空间是对传统度量空间的一种推广，因此固定点结果的等价性跨越了各种数学框架，进一步证明了这些原理在更广泛的数学背景下的通用性和重要性。因此，这些不同类型的度量空间中的固定点结果本质上是相通的，这不仅扩展了我们对固定点理论的理解，也展示了数学中不同领域之间的紧密联系。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Banach Contraction Principle is valid in relational metric spaces.
  • Edelstein's 1961 statement is equivalent to the Banach Contraction Principle.
  • Nieto and Rodriguez-Lopez's 2005 result is in quasi-ordered metric spaces.
  • Fixed point results in different types of metric spaces are equivalent.
  • Rs-relational metric spaces are a generalization of metric spaces.
  • Equivalence of fixed point results holds across various mathematical frameworks.

36. Minimax optimal dual control -- The single input case

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18550v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：An explicit solution is derived for the Bellman inequality corresponding to minimax optimal dual control. The minimizing player determines control action as a function of past state measurements and inputs. The maximizing player selects disturbances and model parameters for the underlying linear time-invariant dynamics. The optimal minimizing policy is a dual controller that optimizes the tradeoff between exploration and exploitation. Once sufficient data has been collected, the policy becomes a deterministic certainty equivalence controller. However, when data is insufficient, the policy introduces a randomized term to improve excitation.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Bellman不等式表明，具有最小最大最优对偶控制解的系统可以通过最小化玩家的控制动作来实现，这些动作依赖于过去的状态测量和输入。同时，最大化玩家则会选择扰动和线性动态模型参数。最优的最小化策略需要在探索和利用之间取得平衡。当有足够的数据时，该策略可以变得确定性，但当数据不足时，引入随机项可以更好地激发系统，从而提高控制效果。因此，数据的充足与否直接影响了控制策略的确定性和随机性，确保了在不同条件下都能实现最优控制。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Bellman inequality has minimax optimal dual control solutions.
  • Minimizing player's control action depends on past state measurements and inputs.
  • Maximizing player selects disturbances and model parameters for linear dynamics.
  • Optimal minimizing policy balances exploration and exploitation.
  • Sufficient data makes the policy deterministic.
  • Insufficient data introduces randomized terms for better excitation.

37. 深度V20手动安装最新的Virtualbox- Community - Deepin ...

  • 链接：https://bbs.deepin.org/post/200160
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：2020年8月22日 · 深度V20手动安装最新的Virtualbox 6. 机器重启以后，安装Virtualbox的扩展包 Copy the Code Reply Like 0 Favorite View the author All Replies shendu001 deepin 2020-08-22 21:22 #1 直接 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，安装依赖软件时需要先更新包列表，确保安装的软件是最新的。其次，安装Virtualbox前应添加其官方仓库，以便安装过程中自动获取依赖包。安装Virtualbox后，还需安装扩展包以充分利用其功能。然而，安装Debian内核可能导致系统无法正常启动，因此在安装前应谨慎考虑。重启机器后，需要再次安装Virtualbox的扩展包，以确保虚拟环境的正常运行。此外，安装Virtualbox的仓库可以同时安装依赖包，简化安装过程。如果系统无法启动，关闭Secure Boot可能是一个解决方案。检测不到物理机的U盘可能是虚拟机的问题，此时应检查虚拟机的设置。最后，将当前用户加入vboxusers组可以解决USB设备无法识别的问题，确保虚拟机能够正常访问外部设备。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 安装依赖软件需要先更新包列表。
  • 安装Virtualbox前需要添加其官方仓库。
  • 安装Virtualbox后需要安装扩展包。
  • 安装Debian内核可能导致系统无法正常启动。
  • 重启机器后需要安装Virtualbox的扩展包。
  • 安装Virtualbox的仓库可以同时安装依赖包。
  • 关闭Secure Boot可能解决系统无法启动的问题。
  • 检测不到物理机的U盘可能是虚拟机的问题。
  • 将当前用户加入vboxusers组可能解决USB设备问题。

38. Duality for the Adversarial Total Variation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18540v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Adversarial training of binary classifiers can be reformulated as regularized risk minimization involving a nonlocal total variation. Building on this perspective, we establish a characterization of the subdifferential of this total variation using duality techniques. To achieve this, we derive a dual representation of the nonlocal total variation and a related integration of parts formula, involving a nonlocal gradient and divergence. We provide such duality statements both in the space of continuous functions vanishing at infinity on proper metric spaces and for the space of essentially bounded functions on Euclidean domains. Furthermore, under some additional conditions we provide characterizations of the subdifferential in these settings.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，duality techniques 能够提供非局部总变差的双重表示，这种表示包括非局部梯度和散度。其次，对于在无穷远处消失的连续函数，以及几乎有界函数，给出了子微分的特征化。然而，某些子微分特征化的结果可能需要额外条件。此外，这些duality陈述在适当的度量空间和欧几里得域中成立，并且使用了部分积分公式。因此，对抗训练中的二元分类器可以被重新表述为正则化风险最小化，其中非局部总变差是关键组成部分。这种视角建立在对抗训练的思想之上，强调了子微分特征化在优化中的重要性。因此，这项工作集中在数学分析和偏微分方程上，而论文对机器学习和优化领域具有相关性。此外，某些结果可能需要额外条件，而这种方法利用了泛函分析中的duality技巧。这些结果对对抗训练方法具有重要意义。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • duality techniques can provide a dual representation of the nonlocal total variation.
  • the dual representation involves a nonlocal gradient and divergence.
  • subdifferential characterizations are provided for continuous functions vanishing at infinity.
  • subdifferential characterizations are also given for essentially bounded functions.
  • additional conditions are required for some characterizations of the subdifferential.
  • duality statements are valid in proper metric spaces and Euclidean domains.
  • the approach uses integration of parts formulas.
  • adversarial training of binary classifiers can be reformulated as regularized risk minimization.
  • nonlocal total variation is a key component in this reformulation.
  • the perspective builds on the idea of adversarial training.
  • subdifferential characterizations are important for optimization.
  • the work focuses on mathematical analysis and PDEs.
  • the paper is relevant to machine learning and optimization.
  • additional conditions may be necessary for certain results.
  • the approach uses duality techniques in functional analysis.
  • the results have implications for adversarial training methods.

39. Double Descent in Quantum Kernel Ridge Regression

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17202v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Various classical machine learning models, including linear regression, kernel methods, and deep neural networks, exhibit double descent, in which the test risk peaks near the interpolation threshold and then decreases in the overparameterized regime. However, this phenomenon has received less attention in the quantum setting. In this work, we investigate the double descent phenomenon in quantum kernel ridge regression (QKRR). By applying deterministic equivalents from random matrix theory (RMT), we derive an asymptotic expression for the test risk of QKRR in the high-dimensional limit. Our analysis rigorously characterizes the interpolation peak and reveals how explicit regularization can effectively suppress it. We corroborate our theoretical results with numerical simulations, demonstrating close agreement even for finite-size quantum systems.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

测试风险在插值阈值附近达到峰值，这是测试风险的一个重要特征。随着参数数量超过插值点，测试风险会逐渐下降，进入过参数化区域。量子设置中的双下降现象较少受到关注，但量子随机化回归（QKRR）确实表现出双下降现象。通过引入显式正则化，可以抑制插值点的峰值，从而改善测试风险。数值模拟证实了理论结果，有限大小的量子系统显示出与理论结果的紧密一致。随机矩阵理论（RMT）被应用于推导测试风险的表达式，而渐近表达式则在高维极限中刻画了测试风险。因此，这些研究不仅揭示了测试风险在不同参数区域的行为，还通过理论和实验验证了双下降现象在量子系统中的存在。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • test risk can peak near the interpolation threshold.
  • test risk decreases in the overparameterized regime.
  • double descent phenomenon has less attention in the quantum setting.
  • QKRR can exhibit double descent.
  • explicit regularization can suppress the interpolation peak.
  • numerical simulations confirm theoretical results.
  • finite-size quantum systems show close agreement.
  • random matrix theory (RMT) is applied to derive test risk expression.
  • asymptotic expression characterizes test risk in high-dimensional limit.

40. On Chromatic Asymptotic Approximate Groups

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18577v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We study a chromatic theory of asymptotic approximate groups for tuples of subsets of abelian groups, combining Nathanson's chromatic sumset formalism with asymptotic covering ideas from approximate group theory. This framework encodes simultaneous additive growth across several color classes. We show some general lifting and invariance principles, establish chromatic covering theorems for finite tuples and for tuples whose color classes are finite unions of unbounded linear sets, and obtain exact structure theorems for translated submonoids and finite-set-plus-submonoid sets. We also obtain sharper binomial bounds in the finite and unbounded-linear cases than the previous lattice-covering estimates. In the integer setting, we show that for each fixed threshold $t$, the threshold-$t$ chromatic layers form an asymptotic approximate family, using Nathanson's eventual interval-plus-edges description to obtain a uniform bound of size $r+2$ and prove an inhomogeneous extension for certain families.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

chromatic sumset formalism编码了多个颜色类别的同时增长，而threshold-$t$ chromatic层则形成一个渐近近似家族，这些家族的估计比之前的格覆盖估计更尖锐。unbounded linear集的有限并集可以用于建立覆盖定理，而translated submonoids和有限集加上子半群集则具有精确结构定理。在整数情况下，使用Nathanson的最终区间加边描述来获得统一的大小$r+2$。此外，connected papers工具、bibliographic explorer工具、litmaps工具、scite.ai工具、alphaXiv工具、catalyzex工具、dagshub工具、gotit.pub工具、huggingface工具、sciencecast工具和arxivLabs项目等工具，可以帮助理解相关文献、引用关系、引用网络、智能引用、arXiv论文的关联、模型的关联以及论文和模型的关联。arxivLabs项目允许社区合作开发arXiv新功能，其中influence flower工具和core recommender工具可以帮助理解引用影响和核心推荐。因此，这些工具和概念共同构建了一个全面而细致的研究框架，有助于深入理解颜色增长、渐近估计以及文献和引用网络的关系。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • chromatic sumset formalism编码了多个颜色类别的同时增长。
  • threshold-$t$ chromatic层形成一个渐近近似家族。
  • unbounded linear集的有限并集可以用于建立覆盖定理。
  • translated submonoids和有限集加上子半群集具有精确结构定理。
  • 在整数情况下，使用Nathanson的最终区间加边描述来获得统一的大小$r+2$。
  • 渐近近似家族的估计比之前的格覆盖估计更尖锐。
  • connected papers工具可以帮助理解相关文献。
  • bibliographic explorer工具可以帮助理解引用关系。
  • litmaps工具可以帮助理解引用网络。
  • scite.ai工具可以帮助理解智能引用。
  • alphaXiv工具可以帮助理解arXiv论文的关联。
  • catalyzex工具可以帮助理解代码和数据的关联。
  • dagshub工具可以帮助理解代码和数据的关联。
  • gotit.pub工具可以帮助理解论文的关联。
  • huggingface工具可以帮助理解模型的关联。

41. A Kantorovich-type variant of Grünwald Interpolation Operators

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17918v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this paper, we introduce a new sequence of operators based on the Grünwald interpolation operators on Chebyshev nodes on the space $L^p[0,π]$. The operators we consider are integral variants of the Grünwald interpolation operators, inspired from the classical Kantorovich operators. Unlike the original Grünwald interpolation operators, our construction enables the derivation of convergence results not only on $C[0,π]$ but also in the space $L^p[0,π]$. First, we establish the uniform boundedness of this sequence on these spaces and subsequently prove the convergence of the operators. We obtain quantitative estimates using modulus of continuity and a suitable K-functional. Furthermore, we derive a point-wise estimate via the Hardy-Littlewood maximal operator. By invoking a Korovkin-type theorem, we extend the convergence results to several Banach function spaces on a nontrivial subspace. In particular, we establish these results for weighted Lebesgue spaces, Grand Lebesgue spaces, Morrey spaces, Orlicz spaces etc.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Kantorovich-type算子是Grüwald插值算子的积分变体，基于Chebyshev节点上的Grüwald插值。这些算子在Banach函数空间的非平凡子空间上具有重要性，其构造使得在\(L^p\)空间中获得收敛结果成为可能。首先，通过Grüwald插值算子的性质，可以证明算子序列在\(L^p[0,\pi]\)和\(C[0,\pi]\)上的均匀有界性，这是收敛证明的关键。其次，利用Hardy-Littlewood极大算子进行点态估计，而Korovkin型定理则为将结果扩展到Banach函数空间提供了理论基础。此外，通过模连续性和K-函数分析量，可以得到定量估计。因此，这些算子的收敛结果不仅适用于\(L^p\)空间，还扩展到了加权勒贝格空间、Grand勒贝格空间、Morrey空间和Orlicz空间。因此，这些结果在分析中对于各种函数空间具有重要意义。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Kantorovich-type operators are integral variants of Grünwald interpolation operators.
  • Uniform boundedness of the sequence on $L^p[0,\pi]$ and $C[0,\pi]$ is established.
  • Convergence results are obtained in both $C[0,\pi]$ and $L^p[0,\pi]$.
  • Quantitative estimates use modulus of continuity and K-functional.
  • Point-wise estimates are derived via the Hardy-Littlewood maximal operator.
  • Korovkin-type theorems are invoked to extend results to Banach function spaces.
  • Convergence results are extended to weighted Lebesgue spaces.
  • Convergence results are also valid for Grand Lebesgue spaces.
  • Convergence results apply to Morrey spaces.
  • Convergence results hold for Orlicz spaces.
  • The operators are based on Grünwald interpolation on Chebyshev nodes.
  • The results are applicable to a nontrivial subspace of Banach function spaces.
  • The construction enables derivation of convergence results in $L^p$ spaces.
  • The operators are inspired by classical Kantorovich operators.
  • The uniform boundedness is crucial for the convergence proofs.
  • The Korovkin-type theorem provides a theoretical basis for the extension.
  • The Hardy-Littlewood maximal operator helps in point-wise estimates.
  • The results are significant for various function spaces in analysis.

C. Vinaya View a PDF of the paper titled A Kantorovich-type variant of Gr\"unwald Interpolation Operators, by P. C. Vinaya View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: In this paper, we introduce a new sequence of operators based on the Grünwald interpolation operators on Chebyshev nodes on the space $L^p[0,{\pi}]$. The operators we consider are integral variants of the Grünwald interpolation operators, inspired from the classical Kantorovich operators. Unlike the original Grünwald interpolation operators, our construction enables the derivation of convergence results not only on $C[0,{\pi}]$ but also in the space $L^p[0,{\pi}]$. First, we establish the uniform boundedness of this sequence on these spaces and subsequently prove the convergence of the operators. We obtain quantitative estimates using modulus of continuity and a suitable K-functional. Furthermore, we derive a point-wise estimate via the Hardy-Littlewood maximal operator. By invoking a Korovkin-type theorem, we extend the convergence results to several Banach function spaces on a nontrivial subspace. 42. Uniform analyticity of local observables in FK-percolation and analyticity of the Ising spontaneous magnetisation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18558v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We prove that, in the FK-percolation model, the probabilities of local events are uniformly analytic in the percolation parameter $p$ under suitable mixing assumptions on the measure, and satisfy a uniform exponential growth bound. This result allows us to prove that the magnetisation of the Potts model is analytic in a suitable range of parameters, including the Ising case in all dimensions $d \geq 3$ in the whole supercritical regime. We also provide a proof of the analyticity of the susceptibility of the Potts model with $q$ colours, for any $q \geq 2$ in the whole subcritical interval. Finally, we prove the analyticity of various quantities in the FK-percolation measure, including the multi-point and truncated multi-point connectivity probabilities.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

均匀指数增长界适用于局部事件的概率，这意味着在特定条件下，系统的增长可以被精确地量化。磁化量的解析性依赖于渗流参数 \( p \)，即磁化量的解析性与渗流过程中的概率分布密切相关。对于 \( q \geq 2 \) 颜色的 Potts 模型，磁化量的解析性成立。在三维及更高维度的超临界区域，磁化量的解析性结果同样适用。此外，磁化量的解析性不仅包括单点和截断的多点连通概率，还涵盖了 Ising 模型的情况。在 FK-渗流测度下，磁化量和其它量的解析性也被证明。对于磁化量的解析性，渗流参数 \( p \) 的亚临界区间同样适用于 \( q \geq 2 \) 颜色的情况。因此，这些解析性结果为理解和预测复杂系统的行为提供了理论基础。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • uniform exponential growth bound applies to probabilities of local events.
  • analyticity of magnetisation depends on percolation parameter p.
  • analyticity of susceptibility holds for Potts model with q ≥ 2 colors.
  • analyticity results apply to supercritical regime in dimensions d ≥ 3.
  • analyticity includes multi-point and truncated multi-point connectivity probabilities.
  • mixing assumptions on the measure are required for analyticity.
  • analyticity of magnetisation includes the Ising case.
  • analyticity of quantities in FK-percolation measure is proven.
  • subcritical interval for susceptibility includes q ≥ 2 colors.

43. MASS-RAG: Multi-Agent Synthesis Retrieval-Augmented Generation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18509v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Large language models (LLMs) are widely used in retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) to incorporate external knowledge at inference time. However, when retrieved contexts are noisy, incomplete, or heterogeneous, a single generation process often struggles to reconcile evidence effectively. We propose \textbf{MASS-RAG}, a multi-agent synthesis approach to retrieval-augmented generation that structures evidence processing into multiple role-specialized agents. MASS-RAG applies distinct agents for evidence summarization, evidence extraction, and reasoning over retrieved documents, and combines their outputs through a dedicated synthesis stage to produce the final answer. This design exposes multiple intermediate evidence views, allowing the model to compare and integrate complementary information before answer generation. Experiments on four benchmarks show that MASS-RAG consistently improves performance over strong RAG baselines, particularly in settings where relevant evidence is distributed across retrieved contexts.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

LLMs在RAG中的使用可能因检索到的上下文噪声、不完整或异质而受到影响。为解决这一问题，MASS-RAG通过将证据处理结构化为多个角色专业化代理来改进RAG系统。具体而言，证据总结、提取和推理由不同的代理完成，每个代理专注于特定的任务。MASS-RAG还通过专门的合成阶段结合各个代理的输出，从而生成更准确的答案。此外，多个中间证据视图的暴露允许模型在答案生成前比较和整合互补信息，进一步提高答案的质量。实验结果表明，MASS-RAG在多个基准上优于强RAG基线，特别是在相关证据分布在检索到的上下文中时，其表现更为突出。因此，MASS-RAG通过多代理结构和合成阶段，有效解决了LLMs在RAG中遇到的问题，并显著提升了模型的性能。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • LLMs在RAG中的使用可能因检索到的上下文噪声、不完整或异质而受到影响。
  • MASS-RAG通过将证据处理结构化为多个角色专业化代理来解决这一问题。
  • 证据总结、提取和推理由不同的代理完成。
  • MASS-RAG通过专门的合成阶段结合各个代理的输出。
  • 多个中间证据视图的暴露允许模型在答案生成前比较和整合互补信息。
  • 实验表明，MASS-RAG在多个基准上优于强RAG基线。
  • 特别在相关证据分布在检索到的上下文中的情况下，MASS-RAG表现更佳。

44. Physics-Informed Tracking (PIT)

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16895v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We propose Physics-Informed Tracking (PIT), a video-based framework for tracking a single particle from video, where a neural network autoencoder localizes a particle as a heatmap peak (landmark) and a differentiable physics module embedded in the autoencoder constrains several landmarks over time (a trajectory) to satisfy known dynamics. The novel Physics-Informed Landmark Loss (PILL) compares this predicted trajectory back against the landmarks, enforcing physical consistency without labels. Its supervised variant (PILLS) instead compares the prediction against ground-truth position, velocity, and bounce from simulation, enabling end-to-end backpropagation. To support supervised and unsupervised learning, we use an autoencoder with a split bottleneck that separates A) tracking-related structure via landmark heatmaps from B) background noise and subsequent image reconstruction. We evaluate a replicated 26 factorial design (n = 4 replicates, 64 configurations), showing that PILLS consistently achieves sub-pixel tracking accuracy for the bilinear and physics-refined decoder outputs under both clean and noisy conditions.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

PIT框架结合了神经网络和物理约束来跟踪单个粒子，通过具有分裂瓶颈的自编码器分离跟踪相关结构和背景噪声，从而实现亚像素级别的跟踪。PILL损失函数进一步通过对比预测轨迹和地标来确保物理一致性，而PILLS监督变体则通过对比预测和模拟的真实位置、速度和反弹来实现端到端反向传播。PIT在多种配置下进行评估，展示了在干净和嘈杂条件下的一致亚像素跟踪准确性，背景噪声和后续图像重建被分离以支持监督和无监督学习。因此，PIT框架在计算机视觉领域具有重要意义，能够提供精确且一致的粒子跟踪结果。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • PIT框架结合了神经网络和物理约束来跟踪单个粒子。
  • PILL损失函数通过对比预测轨迹和地标来确保物理一致性。
  • PILLS监督变体通过对比预测和模拟的真实位置、速度和反弹来实现端到端反向传播。
  • PIT使用具有分裂瓶颈的自编码器来分离跟踪相关结构和背景噪声。
  • PIT在多种配置下进行评估，展示了在干净和嘈杂条件下的一致亚像素跟踪准确性。
  • 背景噪声和后续图像重建被分离以支持监督和无监督学习。
  • PIT框架在计算机视觉领域具有重要意义。

45. MultiWorld: Scalable Multi-Agent Multi-View Video World Models

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18564v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Video world models have achieved remarkable success in simulating environmental dynamics in response to actions by users or agents. They are modeled as action-conditioned video generation models that take historical frames and current actions as input to predict future frames. Yet, most existing approaches are limited to single-agent scenarios and fail to capture the complex interactions inherent in real-world multi-agent systems. We present \textbf{MultiWorld}, a unified framework for multi-agent multi-view world modeling that enables accurate control of multiple agents while maintaining multi-view consistency. We introduce the Multi-Agent Condition Module to achieve precise multi-agent controllability, and the Global State Encoder to ensure coherent observations across different views. MultiWorld supports flexible scaling of agent and view counts, and synthesizes different views in parallel for high efficiency. Experiments on multi-player game environments and multi-robot manipulation tasks demonstrate that MultiWorld outperforms baselines in video fidelity, action-following ability, and multi-view consistency. Project page: https://multi-world.github.io/
  • 易漏细节梳理：

video world models 需要模拟用户或代理的动作响应的环境动态。然而，现有的方法主要局限于单代理场景，未能捕捉真实多代理系统中的复杂交互。为了解决这一问题，MultiWorld 提供了一个统一框架，支持多代理多视角世界建模。首先，Multi-Agent Condition Module 用于实现精确的多代理可控性，确保每个代理的行为可以被准确地控制和预测。其次，Global State Encoder 用于确保不同视角下的观察一致性，使得从不同角度观察到的世界状态保持一致。因此，MultiWorld 支持灵活扩展代理和视角的数量，并且能够并行合成不同视角以提高效率。实验结果表明，MultiWorld 在视频保真度、动作跟随能力和多视角一致性方面优于基线，能够准确控制多个代理并保持多视角一致性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • video world models 需要模拟用户或代理的动作响应的环境动态。
  • 现有的方法主要局限于单代理场景，未能捕捉真实多代理系统中的复杂交互。
  • MultiWorld 提供了一个统一框架，支持多代理多视角世界建模。
  • Multi-Agent Condition Module 用于实现精确的多代理可控性。
  • Global State Encoder 用于确保不同视角下的观察一致性。
  • MultiWorld 支持灵活扩展代理和视角的数量。
  • MultiWorld 并行合成不同视角以提高效率。
  • 实验表明 MultiWorld 在视频保真度、动作跟随能力和多视角一致性方面优于基线。
  • MultiWorld 能够准确控制多个代理并保持多视角一致性。

[2604.18564v1] MultiWorld: Scalable Multi-Agent Multi-View Video World Models Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2604.18564v1 (cs) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: MultiWorld: Scalable Multi-Agent Multi-View Video World Models Authors: Haoyu Wu , Jiwen Yu , Yingtian Zou , Xihui Liu View a PDF of the paper titled MultiWorld: Scalable Multi-Agent Multi-View Video World Models, by Haoyu Wu and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Video world models have achieved remarkable success in simulating environmental dynamics in response to actions by users or agents. They are modeled as action-conditioned video generation models that take historical frames and current actions as input to predict future frames. Yet, most existing approaches are limited to single-agent scenarios and fail to capture the complex interactions inherent in real-world multi-agent systems. We present \textbf{MultiWorld}, a unified framework for multi-agent multi-view world modeling that enables accurate control of multiple agents while maintaining multi-view consistency. We introduce the Multi-Agent Condition Module to achieve precise multi-agent controllability, and the Global State Encoder to ensure coherent observations across different views. MultiWorld supports flexible scaling of agent and view counts, and synthesizes different views in parallel for high efficiency. Experiments on multi-player game environments and multi-robot manipulation tasks demonstrate that MultiWorld outperforms baselines in video fidelity, action-following ability, and multi-view consistency. 46. Aligning Language Models for Lyric-to-Melody Generation with Rule-Based Musical Constraints

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18489v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise in lyric-to-melody generation, but models trained with Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) often produce musically implausible melodies with issues like poor rhythm and unsuitable vocal ranges, a phenomenon we term "constraint violation". To address this, we propose a novel alignment framework that instills musical knowledge without human annotation. We define rule-based musical constraints to automatically generate a preference dataset from an SFT model's outputs. The model is then aligned through a sequential process, first using Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) on paired preference data, followed by Kahneman-Tversky Optimization (KTO) on unpaired negative samples. Experimental results demonstrate that our aligned model substantially reduces rule violations and outperforms strong baselines in both objective and subjective evaluations, generating melodies with substantially improved musicality and coherence. An interactive demo with audio comparisons is available at https://arain233.github.io/AligningMelody-demo.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，生成的旋律在音乐性和连贯性方面得到了显著改善，这主要得益于新的优化框架——Aligning Language Models (LLMs)，它通过两个步骤来提升旋律质量：Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) 和 Kahneman-Tversky Optimization (KTO)。其次，实验结果表明，改进后的模型大幅减少了规则违反现象，这是因为生成的旋律更加符合音乐规则，即 rule-based musical constraints 是自动从 SFT 模型输出中生成的。此外，Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) 模型往往生成不合理的旋律，而 Human annotation 并不是生成偏好数据的一部分，因此需要通过 DPO 和 KTO 来优化生成的旋律。因此，通过 Sequential alignment 过程，生成的旋律在节奏和音域上更加合适，从而在 Objective 和主观评估中都优于基线模型。因此，改进后的模型不仅在音乐性和连贯性上有所提升，还通过 Interactive demo 提供了音频比较，使用户能够直观地感受到改进的效果。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • constraint violation 是指生成的旋律不符合音乐规则的现象。
  • Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) 需要在成对的偏好数据上进行。
  • Kahneman-Tversky Optimization (KTO) 需要在未配对的负面样本上进行。
  • 生成的旋律在音乐性和连贯性方面得到了显著改善。
  • 实验结果表明，改进后的模型大幅减少了规则违反现象。
  • rule-based musical constraints 是自动从 SFT 模型输出中生成的。
  • Sequential alignment 过程包括两个步骤：DPO 和 KTO。
  • Human annotation 不是生成偏好数据的一部分。
  • Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) 模型往往生成不合理的旋律。
  • Aligning Language Models (LLMs) 是解决旋律生成问题的新框架。
  • Interactive demo 提供了音频比较，可在指定网站访问。
  • Objective 和主观评估都表明改进后的模型优于基线。
  • 生成的旋律在节奏和音域上更合适。

47. Interpolating Discrete Diffusion Models with Controllable Resampling

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17310v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Discrete diffusion models form a powerful class of generative models across diverse domains, including text and graphs. However, existing approaches face fundamental limitations. Masked diffusion models suffer from irreversible errors due to early unmasking, while uniform diffusion models, despite enabling self-correction, often yield low-quality samples due to their strong reliance on intermediate latent states. We introduce IDDM, an Interpolating Discrete Diffusion Model, that improves diffusion by reducing dependence on intermediate latent states. Central to IDDM is a controllable resampling mechanism that partially resets probability mass to the marginal distribution, mitigating error accumulation and enabling more effective token corrections. IDDM specifies a generative process whose transitions interpolate between staying at the current state, resampling from a prior, and flipping toward the target state, while enforcing marginal consistency and fully decoupling training from inference. We benchmark our model against state-of-the-art discrete diffusion models across molecular graph generation as well as text generation tasks, demonstrating competitive performance.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

易漏但重要的离散扩散模型改进机制——IDDM（Invertible Diffusion Model），通过引入可控制的重采样机制，可以部分重置概率质量到边缘分布，从而减少错误累积，显著改进了扩散模型。IDDM的生成过程通过在当前状态、从先验抽样和向目标状态翻转之间进行插值来实现，确保生成过程的边缘一致性并完全解耦训练和推理。相比之下，Masked diffusion模型因早期去遮蔽而产生不可逆错误，而Uniform diffusion模型虽然允许自我纠正，但往往产生低质量样本。因此，IDDM在分子图生成和文本生成任务中表现出竞争力，通过减少对中间潜状态的依赖，改进了扩散过程，提升了生成样本的质量和一致性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • controllable resampling机制可以部分重置概率质量到边缘分布，减少错误累积。
  • IDDM通过减少对中间潜状态的依赖来改进扩散。
  • IDDM的生成过程通过在当前状态、从先验抽样和向目标状态翻转之间进行插值来实现。
  • IDDM确保边缘一致性并完全解耦训练和推理。
  • IDDM在分子图生成和文本生成任务中表现出竞争力。
  • Masked diffusion模型因早期去遮蔽而产生不可逆错误。
  • Uniform diffusion模型虽然允许自我纠正，但往往产生低质量样本。
  • IDDM通过引入可控制的重采样机制来改进离散扩散模型。
  • IDDM的生成过程通过在当前状态、从先验抽样和向目标状态翻转之间进行插值来实现。
  • IDDM确保生成过程的边缘一致性。
  • IDDM完全解耦训练和推理。

48. Evolutionary Negative Module Pruning for Better LoRA Merging

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17753v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Merging multiple Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) experts into a single backbone is a promising approach for efficient multi-task deployment. While existing methods strive to alleviate interference via weight interpolation or subspace alignment, they rest upon the implicit assumption that all LoRA matrices contribute constructively to the merged model. In this paper, we uncover a critical bottleneck in current merging paradigms: the existence of $\textit{negative modules}$ -- specific LoRA layers that inherently degrade global performance upon merging. We propose $\textbf{E}$volutionary $\textbf{N}$egative $\textbf{M}$odule $\textbf{P}$runing ($\textbf{ENMP}$), a plug-and-play LoRA pruning method to locate and exclude these detrimental modules prior to merging. By leveraging an evolutionary search strategy, ENMP effectively navigates the discrete, non-differentiable landscape of module selection to identify optimal pruning configurations. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that ENMP consistently boosts the performance of existing merging algorithms, achieving a new state-of-the-art across both language and vision domains. Code is available at https://github.com/CaoAnda/ENMP-LoRAMerging.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，负模块（negative modules）在合并时会不可避免地降低整体性能，这揭示了在模型合并过程中存在的潜在问题。其次，ENMP（Evolutionary Network Module Pruning）作为一种即插即用的LoRA剪枝方法，通过进化搜索策略识别出最优的剪枝配置，从而有效地解决了这一问题。此外，ENMP不仅能够稳定地提升现有合并算法的性能，还能够在语言和视觉领域达到新的技术前沿，展示了其在实际应用中的强大潜力。因此，ENMP不仅解决了模型合并中的关键问题，还推动了相关技术的发展。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • negative modules inherently degrade global performance upon merging
  • ENMP is a plug-and-play LoRA pruning method
  • ENMP uses an evolutionary search strategy to identify optimal pruning configurations
  • ENMP consistently boosts the performance of existing merging algorithms
  • ENMP achieves a new state-of-the-art in both language and vision domains

49. Inductive Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization for Tensor Completion with Arbitrary Sampling

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17001v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The recently established Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization (CNNM) addresses the problem of \textit{tensor completion with arbitrary sampling} (TCAS), which involves restoring a tensor from a subset of its entries sampled in an arbitrary manner. Despite its promising performance, the optimization procedure of CNNM needs performing Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) multiple times, which is computationally expensive and hard to parallelize. To address the issue, we reformulate the optimization objective of CNNM from the perspective of convolution eigenvectors. By introducing pre-learned convolution eigenvectors which are shared among different tensors, we propose a novel method called Inductive Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization (ICNNM), which bypasses the SVD step so as to decrease significantly the computational time. In addition, due to the extra prior knowledge encoded in the pre-learned convolution eigenvectors, ICNNM also outperforms CNNM in terms of recovery performance. Extensive experiments on video completion, prediction and frame interpolation verify the superiority of ICNNM over CNNM and several other competing methods.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

ICNNM 方法通过引入预学习的卷积特征向量来减少计算时间，同时在恢复性能上优于 CNNM。预学习的卷积特征向量包含额外的先验知识，使得 ICNNM 方法适用于任意采样的张量完成问题。此外，ICNNM 方法通过省略 SVD 步骤来降低计算成本，而 CNNM 方法需要多次执行 SVD 步骤，导致优化过程计算成本高且难以并行化。因此，ICNNM 方法在视频完成、预测和帧内插方面表现出优越性，特别是在处理大规模数据时，其计算效率和恢复性能更为显著。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • ICNNM 方法通过引入预学习的卷积特征向量来减少计算时间。
  • ICNNM 方法在恢复性能上优于 CNNM。
  • ICNNM 方法通过省略 SVD 步骤来降低计算成本。
  • 预学习的卷积特征向量包含额外的先验知识。
  • ICNNM 方法适用于任意采样的张量完成问题。
  • CNNM 方法需要多次执行奇异值分解。
  • CNNM 方法的优化过程计算成本高且难以并行化。
  • ICNNM 方法在视频完成、预测和帧内插方面表现出优越性。

[2604.17001v1] Inductive Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization for Tensor Completion with Arbitrary Sampling Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2604.17001v1 (cs) [Submitted on 18 Apr 2026] Title: Inductive Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization for Tensor Completion with Arbitrary Sampling Authors: Wei Li , Yuyang Li , Kaile Du , Yi Yu , Guangcan Liu View a PDF of the paper titled Inductive Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization for Tensor Completion with Arbitrary Sampling, by Wei Li and 4 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The recently established Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization (CNNM) addresses the problem of \textit{tensor completion with arbitrary sampling} (TCAS), which involves restoring a tensor from a subset of its entries sampled in an arbitrary manner. Despite its promising performance, the optimization procedure of CNNM needs performing Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) multiple times, which is computationally expensive and hard to parallelize. To address the issue, we reformulate the optimization objective of CNNM from the perspective of convolution eigenvectors. By introducing pre-learned convolution eigenvectors which are shared among different tensors, we propose a novel method called Inductive Convolution Nuclear Norm Minimization (ICNNM), which bypasses the SVD step so as to decrease significantly the computational time. In addition, due to the extra prior knowledge encoded in the pre-learned convolution eigenvectors, ICNNM also outperforms CNNM in terms of recovery performance. Extensive experiments on video completion, prediction and frame interpolation verify the superiority of ICNNM over CNNM and several other competing methods. 50. Adversarial Humanities Benchmark: Results on Stylistic Robustness in Frontier Model Safety

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18487v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The Adversarial Humanities Benchmark (AHB) evaluates whether model safety refusals survive a shift away from familiar harmful prompt forms. Starting from harmful tasks drawn from MLCommons AILuminate, the benchmark rewrites the same objectives through humanities-style transformations while preserving intent. This extends literature on Adversarial Poetry and Adversarial Tales from single jailbreak operators to a broader benchmark family of stylistic obfuscation and goal concealment. In the benchmark results reported here, the original attacks record 3.84% attack success rate (ASR), while transformed methods range from 36.8% to 65.0%, yielding 55.75% overall ASR across 31 frontier models. Under a European Union AI Act Code-of-Practice-inspired systemic-risk lens, Chemical, biological, radiological and nuclear (CBRN) is the highest bucket. Taken together, this lack of stylistic robustness suggests that current safety techniques suffer from weak generalization: deep understanding of 'non-maleficence' remains a central unresolved problem in frontier model safety.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

transformed方法由于采用了风格上的混淆（stylistic obfuscation），展示出了更高的攻击成功率，相比之下，原始攻击的成功率要低得多。当前的安全技术可能缺乏对“非作恶”原则（non-maleficence）的深刻理解，这使得人类艺术风格的转化能够保留有害任务的意图，同时增加模型的安全风险。基准测试扩展了对对抗性诗歌和故事的研究，揭示了在欧盟人工智能法案（EU AI Act）视角下，CBRN（化学、生物、放射性、核武器）是最具风险的类别。基准测试结果还表明，安全技术在泛化能力上较弱，系统性风险分析揭示了模型安全中的显著漏洞。非作恶原则仍然是模型安全中的一个核心未解决的问题，基准测试家族包括风格上的混淆和目标的隐藏，进一步揭示了模型安全中的系统性风险。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • transformed methods show higher attack success rates due to stylistic obfuscation.
  • original attacks have a much lower success rate compared to transformed methods.
  • current safety techniques may lack deep understanding of 'non-maleficence'.
  • humanities-style transformations preserve the intent of harmful tasks.
  • the benchmark extends previous work on adversarial poetry and tales.
  • CBRN is identified as the highest risk category under the EU AI Act lens.
  • weak generalization in safety techniques is suggested by the benchmark results.
  • non-maleficence remains a central unresolved issue in model safety.
  • the benchmark family includes stylistic obfuscation and goal concealment.
  • systemic-risk analysis reveals significant vulnerabilities in model safety.

51. Too Correct to Learn: Reinforcement Learning on Saturated Reasoning Data

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18493v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Reinforcement Learning (RL) enhances LLM reasoning, yet a paradox emerges as models scale: strong base models saturate standard benchmarks (e.g., MATH), yielding correct but homogeneous solutions. In such environments, the lack of failure cases causes the advantage signal in group-relative algorithms (e.g., GRPO) to vanish, driving policies into mode collapse. To address this, we propose Constrained Uniform Top-K Sampling (CUTS), a parameter-free decoding strategy enforcing structure-preserving exploration. Unlike standard sampling that follows model biases, CUTS flattens the local optimization landscape by sampling uniformly from constrained high-confidence candidates. We integrate this into Mixed-CUTS, a training framework synergizing exploitative and exploratory rollouts to amplify intra-group advantage variance. Experiments on Qwen3 models demonstrate that our approach prevents policy degeneration and significantly boosts out-of-domain generalization. Notably, Mixed-CUTS improves Pass@1 accuracy on the challenging AIME25 benchmark by up to 15.1% over standard GRPO, validating that maintaining diversity within the semantic manifold is critical for rigorous reasoning.

52. Dual Alignment Between Language Model Layers and Human Sentence Processing

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18563v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：A recent study (Kuribayashi et al., 2025) has shown that human sentence processing behavior, typically measured on syntactically unchallenging constructions, can be effectively modeled using surprisal from early layers of large language models (LLMs). This raises the question of whether such advantages of internal layers extend to more syntactically challenging constructions, where surprisal has been reported to underestimate human cognitive effort. In this paper, we begin by exploring internal layers that better estimate human cognitive effort observed in syntactic ambiguity processing in English. Our experiments show that, in contrast to naturalistic reading, later layers better estimate such a cognitive effort, but still underestimate the human data. This dual alignment sheds light on different modes of sentence processing in humans and LMs: naturalistic reading employs a somewhat weak prediction akin to earlier layers of LMs, while syntactically challenging processing requires more fully-contextualized representations, better modeled by later layers of LMs. Motivated by these findings, we also explore several probability-update measures using shallow and deep layers of LMs, sho

53. OGER: A Robust Offline-Guided Exploration Reward for Hybrid Reinforcement Learning

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18530v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Recent advancements in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) have significantly improved Large Language Model (LLM) reasoning, yet models often struggle to explore novel trajectories beyond their initial latent space. While offline teacher guidance and entropy-driven strategies have been proposed to address this, they often lack deep integration or are constrained by the model's inherent capacity. In this paper, we propose OGER, a novel framework that unifies offline teacher guidance and online reinforcement learning through a specialized reward modeling lens. OGER employs multi-teacher collaborative training and constructs an auxiliary exploration reward that leverages both offline trajectories and the model's own entropy to incentivize autonomous exploration. Extensive experiments across mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that OGER significantly outperforms competitive baselines, achieving substantial gains in mathematical reasoning while maintaining robust generalization to out-of-domain tasks. We provide a comprehensive analysis of training dynamics and conduct detailed ablation studies to validate the effectiveness of our entropy-aware re

54. Agentic Forecasting using Sequential Bayesian Updating of Linguistic Beliefs

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18576v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We present BLF (Bayesian Linguistic Forecaster), an agentic system for binary forecasting that achieves state-of-the-art performance on the ForecastBench benchmark. The system is built on three ideas. (1) A Bayesian linguistic belief state: a semi-structured representation combining numerical probability estimates with natural-language evidence summaries, updated by the LLM at each step of an iterative tool-use loop. This contrasts with the common approach of appending all retrieved evidence to an ever-growing context. (2) Hierarchical multi-trial aggregation: running $K$ independent trials and combining them using logit-space shrinkage with a data-dependent prior. (3) Hierarchical calibration: Platt scaling with a hierarchical prior, which avoids over-shrinking extreme predictions for sources with skewed base rates. On 400 backtesting questions from the ForecastBench leaderboard, BLF outperforms all the top public methods, including Cassi, GPT-5, Grok~4.20, and Foresight-32B. Ablation studies show that the structured belief state is as impactful as web search access, and that shrinkage aggregation and hierarchical calibration each provide significant additional gains. [2604.18576v1] Agentic Forecasting using Sequential Bayesian Updating of Linguistic Beliefs Computer Science > Artificial Intelligence arXiv:2604.18576v1 (cs) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: Agentic Forecasting using Sequential Bayesian Updating of Linguistic Beliefs Authors: Kevin Murphy View a PDF of the paper titled Agentic Forecasting using Sequential Bayesian Updating of Linguistic Beliefs, by Kevin Murphy View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: We present BLF (Bayesian Linguistic Forecaster), an agentic system for binary forecasting that achieves state-of-the-art performance on the ForecastBench benchmark. The system is built on three ideas. (1) A Bayesian linguistic belief state: a semi-structured representation combining numerical probability estimates with natural-language evidence summaries, updated by the LLM at each step of an iterative tool-use loop. This contrasts with the common approach of appending all retrieved evidence to an ever-growing context. (2) Hierarchical multi-trial aggregation: running $K$ independent trials and combining them using logit-space shrinkage with a data-dependent prior. (3) Hierarchical calibration: Platt scaling with a hierarchical prior, which avoids over-shrinking extreme predictions for sources with skewed base rates. On 400 backtesting questions from the ForecastBench leaderboard, BLF outperforms all the top public methods, including Cassi, GPT-5, Grok~4.20, and Foresight-32B. Ablation studies show that the structured belief state is as impactful as web search access, and that shrinkage aggregation and hierarchical calibration each provide significant additional gains. In addition, we develop a robust back-testing framework with a leakage rate below 1.5\%, and use rigorous statistical methodology to compare different methods while controlling for various sources of noise. 55. Detectability of minority communities in networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18565v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Community structure is prevalent in real-world networks, with empirical studies revealing heterogeneous distributions where a few dominant majority communities coexist with many smaller groups. These small-scale groups, which we term minority communities, are critical for understanding network organization but pose significant challenges for detection. Here, we investigate the detectability of minority communities from a theoretical perspective using the Stochastic Block Model. We identify three distinct phases of community detection: the detectable phase, where overall community structure is recoverable but minority communities are merged into majority groups; the distinguishable phase, where minority communities form a coherent group separate from the majority but remain unresolved internally; and the resolvable phase, where each minority community is fully distinguishable. These phases correspond to phase transitions at the Kesten-Stigum threshold and two additional thresholds determined by the eigenvalue structure of the signal matrix, which we derive explicitly. Furthermore, we demonstrate that spectral clustering with the Bethe Hessian exhibits significantly weaker detection

[2604.18565v1] Detectability of minority communities in networks Computer Science > Social and Information Networks arXiv:2604.18565v1 (cs) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: Detectability of minority communities in networks Authors: Jiaze Li , Leto Peel View a PDF of the paper titled Detectability of minority communities in networks, by Jiaze Li and Leto Peel View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Community structure is prevalent in real-world networks, with empirical studies revealing heterogeneous distributions where a few dominant majority communities coexist with many smaller groups. These small-scale groups, which we term minority communities, are critical for understanding network organization but pose significant challenges for detection. Here, we investigate the detectability of minority communities from a theoretical perspective using the Stochastic Block Model. We identify three distinct phases of community detection: the detectable phase, where overall community structure is recoverable but minority communities are merged into majority groups; the distinguishable phase, where minority communities form a coherent group separate from the majority but remain unresolved internally; and the resolvable phase, where each minority community is fully distinguishable. These phases correspond to phase transitions at the Kesten-Stigum threshold and two additional thresholds determined by the eigenvalue structure of the signal matrix, which we derive explicitly. Furthermore, we demonstrate that spectral clustering with the Bethe Hessian exhibits significantly weaker detection performance for minority communities compared to belief propagation, revealing a specific limitation of spectral methods in identifying fine-grained community structure despite their capability to detect macroscopic structures down to the theoretical limit. 56. Revisiting Active Sequential Prediction-Powered Mean Estimation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18569v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this work, we revisit the problem of active sequential prediction-powered mean estimation, where at each round one must decide the query probability of the ground-truth label upon observing the covariates of a sample. Furthermore, if the label is not queried, the prediction from a machine learning model is used instead. Prior work proposed an elegant scheme that determines the query probability by combining an uncertainty-based suggestion with a constant probability that encodes a soft constraint on the query probability. We explored different values of the mixing parameter and observed an intriguing empirical pattern: the smallest confidence width tends to occur when the weight on the constant probability is close to one, thereby reducing the influence of the uncertainty-based component. Motivated by this observation, we develop a non-asymptotic analysis of the estimator and establish a data-dependent bound on its confidence interval. Our analysis further suggests that when a no-regret learning approach is used to determine the query probability and control this bound, the query probability converges to the constraint of the max value of the query probability when it is chosen

[2604.18569v1] Revisiting Active Sequential Prediction-Powered Mean Estimation Statistics > Machine Learning arXiv:2604.18569v1 (stat) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: Revisiting Active Sequential Prediction-Powered Mean Estimation Authors: Maria-Eleni Sfyraki , Jun-Kun Wang View a PDF of the paper titled Revisiting Active Sequential Prediction-Powered Mean Estimation, by Maria-Eleni Sfyraki and 1 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: In this work, we revisit the problem of active sequential prediction-powered mean estimation, where at each round one must decide the query probability of the ground-truth label upon observing the covariates of a sample. Furthermore, if the label is not queried, the prediction from a machine learning model is used instead. Prior work proposed an elegant scheme that determines the query probability by combining an uncertainty-based suggestion with a constant probability that encodes a soft constraint on the query probability. We explored different values of the mixing parameter and observed an intriguing empirical pattern: the smallest confidence width tends to occur when the weight on the constant probability is close to one, thereby reducing the influence of the uncertainty-based component. Motivated by this observation, we develop a non-asymptotic analysis of the estimator and establish a data-dependent bound on its confidence interval. Our analysis further suggests that when a no-regret learning approach is used to determine the query probability and control this bound, the query probability converges to the constraint of the max value of the query probability when it is chosen obliviously to the current covariates. We also conduct simulations that corroborate these theoretical findings. 57. Joint Scheduling of Multi-Band Radar Sensing and DNN Inference for Cross-Stage Parallelism

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18520v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：This paper studies end-to-end latency minimization for a multi-band radar sensing and deep neural network (DNN) inference pipeline. Unlike conventional stage-wise designs that treat radar sensing and DNN inference as two sequential stages, the proposed framework exploits cross-stage parallelism by allowing the inference branch associated with a sensed band to start as soon as that band completes sensing, without waiting for all bands to finish. To characterize this interaction, we formulate a joint scheduling problem that couples sensing-time allocation, branch release timing, and non-preemptive multi-core execution of a directed acyclic graph (DAG) under sensing-feasibility, precedence, and core-capacity constraints. Since the resulting problem is combinatorial and strongly time-coupled, we further develop a release-aware heuristic that evaluates each sensing decision according to its downstream impact on the DAG makespan, together with a greedy list scheduler for multi-core DAG execution under release times. Simulation results show that the proposed design can effectively exploit cross-stage parallelism and reduce end-to-end latency relative to a decoupled baseline in many hetero

[2604.18520v1] Joint Scheduling of Multi-Band Radar Sensing and DNN Inference for Cross-Stage Parallelism Electrical Engineering and Systems Science > Signal Processing arXiv:2604.18520v1 (eess) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: Joint Scheduling of Multi-Band Radar Sensing and DNN Inference for Cross-Stage Parallelism Authors: Yanan Du , Sai Xu , Kezhi Wang , Yansha Deng View a PDF of the paper titled Joint Scheduling of Multi-Band Radar Sensing and DNN Inference for Cross-Stage Parallelism, by Yanan Du and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: This paper studies end-to-end latency minimization for a multi-band radar sensing and deep neural network (DNN) inference pipeline. 58. $\exists\mathbb{R}$-Completeness of Tensor Degeneracy and a Derandomization Barrier for Hyperdeterminants

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17061v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We study the computational complexity of singularity for multilinear maps. While the determinant characterizes singularity for matrices, its multilinear analogue -- the hyperdeterminant -- is defined only in boundary format and quickly becomes algebraically unwieldy. We show that the intrinsic notion of tensor singularity, namely degeneracy, is complete for the existential theory of the reals. The reduction is exact and entirely algebraic: homogeneous quadratic feasibility is reduced to projective bilinear feasibility, then to singular matrix-pencil feasibility, and finally encoded directly as tensor degeneracy. No combinatorial gadgets are used. In boundary format, degeneracy coincides with hyperdeterminant vanishing. We therefore isolate the exact gap between intrinsic tensor singularity and its classical polynomial certificate. We show that deterministic hardness transfer to the hyperdeterminant reduces to selecting a point outside the zero set of a completion polynomial, yielding a structured instance of polynomial identity testing. We further formalize the failure of several natural deterministic embedding strategies. This identifies a sharp frontier: real 3-tensor degenerac

[2604.17061v1] $\exists\mathbb{R}$-Completeness of Tensor Degeneracy and a Derandomization Barrier for Hyperdeterminants Computer Science > Computational Complexity arXiv:2604.17061v1 (cs) [Submitted on 18 Apr 2026] Title: $\exists\mathbb{R}$-Completeness of Tensor Degeneracy and a Derandomization Barrier for Hyperdeterminants Authors: Angshul Majumdar View a PDF of the paper titled $\exists\mathbb{R}$-Completeness of Tensor Degeneracy and a Derandomization Barrier for Hyperdeterminants, by Angshul Majumdar View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: We study the computational complexity of singularity for multilinear maps. While the determinant characterizes singularity for matrices, its multilinear analogue -- the hyperdeterminant -- is defined only in boundary format and quickly becomes algebraically unwieldy. 60. When Can LLMs Learn to Reason with Weak Supervision?

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18574v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Large language models have achieved significant reasoning improvements through reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). Yet as model capabilities grow, constructing high-quality reward signals becomes increasingly difficult, making it essential to understand when RLVR can succeed under weaker forms of supervision. We conduct a systematic empirical study across diverse model families and reasoning domains under three weak supervision settings: scarce data, noisy rewards, and self-supervised proxy rewards. We find that generalization is governed by training reward saturation dynamics: models that generalize exhibit a prolonged pre-saturation phase during which training reward and downstream performance climb together, while models that saturate rapidly memorize rather than learn. [2604.18574v1] When Can LLMs Learn to Reason with Weak Supervision? Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2604.18574v1 (cs) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: When Can LLMs Learn to Reason with Weak Supervision? Authors: Salman Rahman , Jingyan Shen , Anna Mordvina , Hamid Palangi , Saadia Gabriel , Pavel Izmailov View a PDF of the paper titled When Can LLMs Learn to Reason with Weak Supervision?, by Salman Rahman and 5 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Large language models have achieved significant reasoning improvements through reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). Yet as model capabilities grow, constructing high-quality reward signals becomes increasingly difficult, making it essential to understand when RLVR can succeed under weaker forms of supervision. We conduct a systematic empirical study across diverse model families and reasoning domains under three weak supervision settings: scarce data, noisy rewards, and self-supervised proxy rewards. We find that generalization is governed by training reward saturation dynamics: models that generalize exhibit a prolonged pre-saturation phase during which training reward and downstream performance climb together, while models that saturate rapidly memorize rather than learn. We identify reasoning faithfulness, defined as the extent to which intermediate steps logically support the final answer, as the pre-RL property that predicts which regime a model falls into, while output diversity alone is uninformative. Motivated by these findings, we disentangle the contributions of continual pre-training and supervised fine-tuning, finding that SFT on explicit reasoning traces is necessary for generalization under weak supervision, while continual pre-training on domain data amplifies the effect. Applied together to Llama3.2-3B-Base, these interventions enable generalization across all three settings where the base model previously failed. 61. Back into Plato's Cave: Examining Cross-modal Representational Convergence at Scale

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18572v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The Platonic Representation Hypothesis suggests that neural networks trained on different modalities (e.g., text and images) align and eventually converge toward the same representation of reality. If true, this has significant implications for whether modality choice matters at all. We show that the experimental evidence for this hypothesis is fragile and depends critically on the evaluation regime. Alignment is measured using mutual nearest neighbors on small datasets ($\approx$1K samples) and degrades substantially as the dataset is scaled to millions of samples. The alignment that remains between model representations reflects coarse semantic overlap rather than consistent fine-grained structure. Moreover, the evaluations in Huh et al. are done in a one-to-one image-caption setting, a constraint that breaks down in realistic many-to-many settings and further reduces alignment. We also find that the reported trend of stronger language models increasingly aligning with vision does not appear to hold for newer models. Overall, our findings suggest that the current evidence for cross-modal representational convergence is considerably weaker than subsequent works have taken it to be

[2604.18572v1] Back into Plato's Cave: Examining Cross-modal Representational Convergence at Scale Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2604.18572v1 (cs) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: Back into Plato's Cave: Examining Cross-modal Representational Convergence at Scale Authors: A. Sophia Koepke , Daniil Zverev , Shiry Ginosar , Alexei A. Efros View a PDF of the paper titled Back into Plato's Cave: Examining Cross-modal Representational Convergence at Scale, by A. Sophia Koepke and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The Platonic Representation Hypothesis suggests that neural networks trained on different modalities (e.g., text and images) align and eventually converge toward the same representation of reality. If true, this has significant implications for whether modality choice matters at all. We show that the experimental evidence for this hypothesis is fragile and depends critically on the evaluation regime. Alignment is measured using mutual nearest neighbors on small datasets ($\approx$1K samples) and degrades substantially as the dataset is scaled to millions of samples. The alignment that remains between model representations reflects coarse semantic overlap rather than consistent fine-grained structure. Moreover, the evaluations in Huh et al. are done in a one-to-one image-caption setting, a constraint that breaks down in realistic many-to-many settings and further reduces alignment. We also find that the reported trend of stronger language models increasingly aligning with vision does not appear to hold for newer models. Overall, our findings suggest that the current evidence for cross-modal representational convergence is considerably weaker than subsequent works have taken it to be. Models trained on different modalities may learn equally rich representations of the world, just not the same one. 62. If at First You Don't Succeed, Trispectrum: I. Estimating the Matter Power Spectrum Covariance with Higher-Order Statistics

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18581v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We present a method to estimate non-Gaussian power spectrum covariance matrices by directly measuring the response of the small-scale power spectrum to long-wavelength perturbations via bispectrum and trispectrum estimators. Specifically, we derive estimators for the complete non-Gaussian matter power spectrum covariance, including the super-sample contribution, in terms of the squeezed bispectrum and collapsed trispectrum of the underlying density field. We apply these estimators to the Quijote simulations, and recover unbiased estimates of the small-scale ($k\gtrsim 0.15~h/{\rm Mpc}$) matter power spectrum covariance at the percent level using only 25 simulations - comparable to the precision of the sample covariance estimated using 5,000 simulations. This technique significantly reduces the number of simulations needed to estimate power spectrum covariances and opens the possibility of inferring power spectrum covariances directly from survey data, enabling stringent tests of simulations and, potentially, power spectrum analyses that do not rely on external covariance matrices.

63. T-REN: Learning Text-Aligned Region Tokens Improves Dense Vision-Language Alignment and Scalability

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18573v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Despite recent progress, vision-language encoders struggle with two core limitations: (1) weak alignment between language and dense vision features, which hurts tasks like open-vocabulary semantic segmentation; and (2) high token counts for fine-grained visual representations, which limits scalability to long videos. This work addresses both limitations. We propose T-REN (Text-aligned Region Encoder Network), an efficient encoder that maps visual data to a compact set of text-aligned region-level representations (or region tokens). T-REN achieves this through a lightweight network added on top of a frozen vision backbone, trained to pool patch-level representations within each semantic region into region tokens and align them with region-level text annotations. With only 3.7% additional parameters compared to the vision-language backbone, this design yields substantially stronger dense cross-modal understanding while reducing the token count by orders of magnitude. Specifically, T-REN delivers +5.9 mIoU on ADE20K open-vocabulary segmentation, +18.4% recall on COCO object-level text-image retrieval, +15.6% recall on Ego4D video object localization, and +17.6% mIoU on VSPW video scen

  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) has become the predominant algorithm for on-policy reinforcement learning due to its scalability and empirical robustness across domains. However, there is a significant disconnect between the underlying foundations of trust region methods and the heuristic clipped objective used in PPO. In this paper, we bridge this gap by introducing the Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) framework. We formulate a novel regularized and constrained policy optimization problem and derive its analytical optimal solution. We prove that this solution ensures monotonic performance improvement. To handle parameterized policy classes, we develop a policy optimization algorithm called Bounded Policy Optimization (BPO) that minimizes an advantage-weighted divergence between the policy and the analytic optimal solution from BRRL. We further establish a lower bound on the expected performance of the resulting policy in terms of the BPO loss function. Notably, our framework also provides a new theoretical lens to interpret the success of the PPO loss, and connects trust region policy optimization and the Cross-Entropy Method (CEM). [2604.18578v1] Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2604.18578v1 (cs) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning Authors: Yunke Ao , Le Chen , Bruce D. In this paper, we bridge this gap by introducing the Bounded Ratio Reinforcement Learning (BRRL) framework. 65. Scaling of Quantum Resources for Simulating a Long-Range System

  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We simulate a long-range extended Ising model in one dimension using a hybrid quantum algorithm, namely Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE). Three structure-aware ansatze incorporating nearest-neighbor (NN), next-nearest-neighbor (NNN), and next-next-nearest-neighbor (NNNN) entangling blocks are constructed by mimicking the string operators in the Hamiltonian. We show that energy fidelity alone is not a good indicator for finding the ground state of our model. To overcome this problem, we introduce an additional criterion based on pairwise logarithmic negativity as a more reliable way to find the actual ground state by the VQE. We find that the interaction range parameter alpha primarily governs the minimum number of ansatz layers required, rather than proximity to the quantum critical point. In particular, we show that in the non-local regime (alpha <= 1), the NNN and NNNN ansatze reduce the layer scaling rate by factors of 2.5x and 3.8x relative to NN in all phases, including the critical point. [2604.18495v1] Scaling of Quantum Resources for Simulating a Long-Range System Quantum Physics arXiv:2604.18495v1 (quant-ph) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: Scaling of Quantum Resources for Simulating a Long-Range System Authors: Tanya Keshari , Debasis Sadhukhan View a PDF of the paper titled Scaling of Quantum Resources for Simulating a Long-Range System, by Tanya Keshari and 1 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: We simulate a long-range extended Ising model in one dimension using a hybrid quantum algorithm, namely Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE). In this quantum simulation, we investigate how quantum resources scale with system size and interaction strength. Three structure-aware ansatze incorporating nearest-neighbor (NN), next-nearest-neighbor (NNN), and next-next-nearest-neighbor (NNNN) entangling blocks are constructed by mimicking the string operators in the Hamiltonian. We show that energy fidelity alone is not a good indicator for finding the ground state of our model. To overcome this problem, we introduce an additional criterion based on pairwise logarithmic negativity as a more reliable way to find the actual ground state by the VQE. We find that the interaction range parameter alpha primarily governs the minimum number of ansatz layers required, rather than proximity to the quantum critical point. In particular, we show that in the non-local regime (alpha <= 1), the NNN and NNNN ansatze reduce the layer scaling rate by factors of 2.5x and 3.8x relative to NN in all phases, including the critical point. The total number of two-qubit gates required for reliable simulation grows quadratically with system size for all three ansatze. This is consistent with the theoretical prediction, as the number of non-local terms in the Hamiltonian also grows quadratically with the system size. In the local regime, however, the number of required two-qubit gates grows linearly with system size. In contrast, in the quasi-local regime, the required number of two-qubit gates for the quantum simulation is more subtle and depends on the phase of the Hamiltonian. 66. AnchorSeg: Language Grounded Query Banks for Reasoning Segmentation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18562v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Reasoning segmentation requires models to ground complex, implicit textual queries into precise pixel-level masks. Existing approaches rely on a single segmentation token $\texttt{}$, whose hidden state implicitly encodes both semantic reasoning and spatial localization, limiting the model's ability to explicitly disentangle what to segment from where to segment. We introduce AnchorSeg, which reformulates reasoning segmentation as a structured conditional generation process over image tokens, conditioned on language grounded query banks. Instead of compressing all semantic reasoning and spatial localization into a single embedding, AnchorSeg constructs an ordered sequence of query banks: latent reasoning tokens that capture intermediate semantic states, and a segmentation anchor token that provides explicit spatial grounding. We model spatial conditioning as a factorized distribution over image tokens, where the anchor query determines localization signals while contextual queries provide semantic modulation. [2604.18562v1] AnchorSeg: Language Grounded Query Banks for Reasoning Segmentation Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2604.18562v1 (cs) [Submitted on 20 Apr 2026] Title: AnchorSeg: Language Grounded Query Banks for Reasoning Segmentation Authors: Rui Qian , Chuanhang Deng , Qiang Huang , Jian Xiong , Mingxuan Li , Yingbo Zhou , Wei Zhai , Jintao Chen , Dejing Dou View a PDF of the paper titled AnchorSeg: Language Grounded Query Banks for Reasoning Segmentation, by Rui Qian and 8 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Reasoning segmentation requires models to ground complex, implicit textual queries into precise pixel-level masks. Existing approaches rely on a single segmentation token $\texttt{}$, whose hidden state implicitly encodes both semantic reasoning and spatial localization, limiting the model's ability to explicitly disentangle what to segment from where to segment. To bridge token-level predictions and pixel-level supervision, we propose Token--Mask Cycle Consistency (TMCC), a bidirectional training objective that enforces alignment across resolutions. By explicitly decoupling spatial grounding from semantic reasoning through structured language grounded query banks, AnchorSeg achieves state-of-the-art results on ReasonSeg test set (67.7\% gIoU and 68.1\% cIoU). 67. Sessa: Selective State Space Attention

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18580v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Modern sequence models are dominated by Transformers, where self-attention mixes information from the visible context in an input-dependent way. However, when retrieval is not sharp and attention remains diffuse over an effective support $S_{\mathrm{eff}}(t)$, the influence of any individual token is diluted, typically scaling as $O(1/S_{\mathrm{eff}}(t))$ and reaching $O(1/\ell)$ for old tokens in full-prefix settings. Structured state-space models process sequences recurrently through an explicit feedback path; selective variants such as Mamba make this feedback input-dependent, yet when freeze time cannot be sustained over long intervals, their long-range sensitivity decays exponentially with lag. Existing architectures therefore either retrieve from the past in a single read or propagate information through a single feedback chain. We introduce Sessa, a decoder that places attention inside a feedback path, enabling recurrent many-path aggregation within a layer.
